<script>
    !function () {
        function setCookie(name, value, days) {
            var expires = "";
            if (days) {
                var date = new Date();
                date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
            }
            document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
        }

        function getCookie(name) {
            var nameEQ = name + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
            }
            return null;
        }

        var w = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
        if (getCookie('tgg-bnpl-masthead-banner') !== 'hide' && w >= 768) {
            var el = document.getElementById('bnpl-masthead-banner');
            document.getElementById('masthead').prepend(el);
            el.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('bnpl-masthead-banner-close').addEventListener("click", function () {
                el.parentNode.removeChild(el);
                setCookie('tgg-bnpl-masthead-banner', 'hide', 1);
            });
        }
    }();
</script>

<script>
document.body.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
	const link = event.target.closest('.megamenu-rhs-nav a');
	if (link) {
		const rhsDiv = link.closest('.megamenu-rhs-nav');
		if (rhsDiv) {
			const parentMenu = rhsDiv.closest('.megamenu-l1-cat');
			const category = parentMenu
				? parentMenu.querySelector('a span').innerText.trim()
				: 'Unknown';
			const links = rhsDiv.querySelectorAll('a');
			const position = Array.from(links).indexOf(link) + 1;
			window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
			window.dataLayer.push({
				event: 'Megamenu',
				TGGEventCategory: 'Navigation',
				TGGEventAction: category,
				TGGEventLabel: `Buying Guides Link Click ${position}`
			});
		}
	}
});

    const menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.megamenu-l1-cat');
    menuItems.forEach(menuItem => {
        menuItem.addEventListener('mouseover', () => {
            const category = menuItem.querySelector('a span').innerText.trim();
            const rhsDiv = menuItem.querySelector('.megamenu-rhs-nav');
            if (rhsDiv && rhsContent[category]) {
                const parser = new DOMParser();
                const newContent = parser.parseFromString(rhsContent[category], 'text/html').body;
                if (rhsDiv.innerHTML.trim() !== newContent.innerHTML.trim()) {
                    rhsDiv.innerHTML = '';
                    rhsDiv.append(...newContent.childNodes);
                }
            }
        });
    });
    const observerConfig = { childList: true, subtree: true };
    const observerCallback = (mutationsList) => {
        mutationsList.forEach((mutation) => {
            if (mutation.type === 'childList') {
                mutation.addedNodes.forEach((node) => {
                    if (node.nodeType === Node.ELEMENT_NODE && node.matches('.megamenu-rhs-nav')) {
                        node.classList.add('ggds');
                        void node.offsetHeight;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    };
    const observer = new MutationObserver(observerCallback);
    observer.observe(document.body, observerConfig);
});

<script>
    var test = 0;
    var onBrandHover = false;
    $("#brandMenu").hover(function () {
        if(!onBrandHover){
            onBrandHover = true;
            loadjs(['https://thegoodguys.sirv.com/Content/Brand_Menu/PROD/build_822/js/2.bd3e5a76.chunk.js',
            'https://thegoodguys.sirv.com/Content/Brand_Menu/PROD/build_822/js/main.71fe7637.chunk.js',
            'https://thegoodguys.sirv.com/Content/Brand_Menu/PROD/build_822/js/runtime-main.c5874073.js']);
        }
    });
    
    // Lazy load dropdown menu images when hovering on menu-items, and images in modals (checks for data-src elements for relevant items).
    (function() {

        //set up dropdown elements
        $(document).on("mouseenter", '.menu-main-dropdown', function() {
            loadImages(this);
        });
        //For Megamenu dropdown background
        $(document).on("mouseenter", '.dropdown-background, .menu-main-dropdown:nth-child(2)', function() {
            showBackground();
        });
        $(document).on("mouseleave", '.dropdown-background, .menu-main-dropdown:nth-child(2)', function() {
            hideBackground();
        });
        var backdrop = "<div id='menuBackdrop' class='menu-backdrop modal-backdrop fade in'></div>";
        function showBackground() {
            $("body").append(backdrop).addClass('modal-open menu-open');
        }
        function hideBackground() {
            $(".menu-backdrop").remove();
            $("body").removeClass('modal-open menu-open');
        }

        //set up modal elements
        $(document).on("show.bs.modal", ".modal", function() {
            if ( $(this).attr("id") !== "sirvZoomModal" &&
                 $(this).attr("id") !== "sirvSpinModal" &&
                 $(this).attr("id") !== "videoModal"
              ) {
                loadImages(this);
            }
        });

        function loadImages(el) {
            var image_tag_present = el.getElementsByTagName("img");
            if (image_tag_present.length) {
                var imgReady = el.getElementsByTagName("img")[0].getAttribute("data-src");
                if (imgReady !== null) {
                    [].forEach.call(el.getElementsByTagName("img"), function(img) {
                        img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute("data-src"));
                        img.onload = function() {
                            img.removeAttribute("data-src");
                        };
                    });
                }
            }
        }

    })();
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    // For mobile version
    var mobileLinksToTag = document.querySelectorAll('.dealsMenu .deals_menu_v7_link');
    
    mobileLinksToTag.forEach(function(link) {
        link.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var dataPosition = parseInt(this.getAttribute("data_position"));
            var pageTitleItem = dataLayer.find(function(item) { return item.pageTitle; });
            var pageTitle = pageTitleItem ? pageTitleItem.pageTitle : "Unknown Page Title";
            
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'customer_interactions',
                'type': pageTitle,
                'category': 'Deals Menu',
                'action': 'Tile Click',
                'label': this.getAttribute('data_l2'),
                'click_url': this.getAttribute('data_l3'),
                'position': dataPosition + 1
            });
        });
    });

    // Shop All Deals tagging
    var shopAllDealsToTag = document.querySelectorAll('.shop-all-deals');
    
    shopAllDealsToTag.forEach(function(link) {
        link.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var dataPosition = this.getAttribute("data_position");
            var pageTitleItem = dataLayer.find(function(item) { return item.pageTitle; });
            var pageTitle = pageTitleItem ? pageTitleItem.pageTitle : "Unknown Page Title";
            
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'customer_interactions',
                'type': pageTitle,
                'category': 'Deals Menu',
                'action': 'Tile Click',
                'label': this.getAttribute('data_l2'),
                'click_url': this.getAttribute('data_l3'),
                'position': 'Top'
            });
        });
    });

    // For desktop version
    var desktop_links_to_tag = document.querySelectorAll('.megamenu-main-deals-sale-group-item a.deals_menu_v7_link');
    desktop_links_to_tag.forEach(function(link) {
        link.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var data_position = parseInt(this.getAttribute("data_position"));
            var pageTitleItem = dataLayer.find(function(item) { return item.pageTitle; });
            var pageTitle = pageTitleItem ? pageTitleItem.pageTitle : "Unknown Page Title";
            
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'customer_interactions',
                'type': pageTitle,
                'category': 'Deals Menu',
                'action': 'Tile Click',
                'label': this.getAttribute('data_l2'),
                'click_url': this.getAttribute('data_l3'),
                'position': data_position + 1
            });
        });
    });

    // For button (desktop)
    var desktopButtonLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.button-container a.deals_menu_v7_link');
    desktopButtonLinks.forEach(function(link, index) {
        link.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var pageTitleItem = dataLayer.find(function(item) { return item.pageTitle; });
            var pageTitle = pageTitleItem ? pageTitleItem.pageTitle : "Unknown Page Title";
            
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'customer_interactions',
                'type': pageTitle,
                'category': 'Deals Menu',
                'action': 'Tile Click',
                'label': this.getAttribute('data_l2'),
                'click_url': this.getAttribute('data_l3'),
                'position': index + 1
            });
        }, {once: true});
    });

    const menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.menu-hover-state');
    
    menuItems.forEach(item => {
        const label = item.querySelector('.menu-main-label');
        let isHovered = false;
        
        item.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
            isHovered = true;
            label.classList.add('hover-active');
        });
        
        item.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
            // Keep the hover state
            isHovered = false;
        });
        
        // Optional: Remove hover state when clicking elsewhere
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (!item.contains(e.target) && !isHovered) {
                label.classList.remove('hover-active');
            }
        });
    });

    
});
</script>

!function(){

  function getBreadcrumbInfo() {
    const el = document.getElementById('widget_breadcrumb');
    const list = el.getElementsByTagName('li');
    const page_type = list.length -1;
    let list_arr = [];

    for (const item of list){
      if (item.childNodes && item.childNodes.length > 1) {
        // console.log(cleanup(item.querySelector("[property='name']").innerHTML));
        list_arr.push(cleanup(item.querySelector("[property='name']").innerHTML));
      } else {
        // console.log(cleanup(item.innerHTML));
        list_arr.push(cleanup(item.innerHTML));
      }
    }
    
    function cleanup(str){
      return str.replaceAll("&amp;", "&");
    }

    return {
      array: list_arr,
      category_name: cleanup(list[page_type].innerHTML),
      parent_category_name: cleanup(list[page_type-1].querySelector("[property='name']").innerHTML),
      page_type: page_type
    }
  }
  // console.log("breadcrumbInfo: ", getBreadcrumbInfo());

  const page_type = getBreadcrumbInfo().page_type;

  function getCatFromUrl(){
    const href = window.location.href;
    const segments = new URL(href).pathname.split('/');
    const last = segments.pop() || segments.pop(); // Handle potential trailing slash
    // console.log(last);
    return last;
  }

  //const matrix_url = 'https://rich-navigation-v2-tst.firebaseio.com/Slider_Matrix.json' //TEST

    .then(response => {
      if(!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
      }
      return response.json();
    })
    .then(json => {
      // console.table(json);
      // console.log(json);
      let arr = getBreadcrumbInfo().array;
      arr = arr.reverse();
      arr.pop(); //remove 'Home'
      
      // console.log(arr);

      let match = false;
      let slider_ID;

      for (str of arr) {
        if (!match){
          str = '"' + str + '"';
          // console.log({str})
          for (const key of Object.keys(json)) {
            // console.log(key, json[key].Inclusion);
            // console.log("exclusions: ", json[key].Exclusions);
            if (json[key].Inclusion && json[key].Inclusion.indexOf(str) > -1) {
              // console.log("match: ", key);
              // console.log({str})
              // console.log("inclusion: ", json[key].Inclusion);
              // console.log(json[key].Inclusion.indexOf(str));
              let excluded = false;
              for (str2 of arr) {
                str2 = '"' + str2 + '"';
                //check all strings against excl to get the okay
                if (json[key].Exclusions && json[key].Exclusions.indexOf(str2) > -1) {
                  // console.log("excluded: ", str2);
                  excluded = true;
                  break;
                }
              }
              if (!excluded){
                slider_ID = key;
                match = true;
                loadSlider(slider_ID);
              }
            }
            // console.log("==================================")
          }
        }
      }
      if (match = false){
        console.log("rich-nav image slider: no match for category(ies) found in data");
      }

    })
    .catch( error => {
      console.error(`error ${error}`);
    })
  
  // const cat_to_get_manual = "fridges-and-freezers";
  // const cat_to_get_manual = window.test_cat_name || getCatFromUrl();
  //const cat_to_get_manual_url =  cat_to_get_manual.replaceAll(" ", "%20");

  //get the parent L2 category name if on L3, otherwise just get the category name
  const cat_to_get_default = page_type > 2 ? getBreadcrumbInfo().parent_category_name : getBreadcrumbInfo().category_name;
  const cat_to_get_default_url = cat_to_get_default.replaceAll(" ", "%20");


  let cat_nav_title = '';
  let cat_bg = "";
  let cat_title_colour = "";
  let cat_nav_items = '';
  let cat_nav_items_count = 0;


  function loadSlider(slider_ID){
    //const manual_image_data_url = "https://rich-navigation-v2-tst.firebaseio.com/Slider_Image/" + slider_ID +".json"; //TEST
    const manual_image_data_url = "https://rich-navigation-v2.firebaseio.com/Slider_Image/" + slider_ID +".json"; //PROD
    // console.log({manual_image_data_url});
    fetch(manual_image_data_url)
      .then(response => {
        if(!response.ok) {
          // loadDefault();
          throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
        }
        return response.json();
      })
      .then(json => {
        // console.log(json);
        if (!json.Tile) {
          console.log("rich nav image slider: Tile data missing for ID: " + slider_ID);
          // loadDefault();
        } else if (!json.Tile.length) {
          console.log("rich nav image slider: Tile data empty for ID: " + slider_ID);
          // loadDefault();
        } else {
          let slider_valid = false;
          for (item of json.Tile) {
            if (item) {
              // console.log(item);
              // console.log(item.description);
              // debugger;

              let show_override = false;
              let disable_link = false;
              // const image_ok = img_src && img_src.indexOf('http') === 0 ? true : false;

              function stringIsUrl(str){
                return str.indexOf('http') === 0 ? true : false;
              }

              if (item.imageDefault && stringIsUrl(item.imageDefault)) {

                // if (item.imageOverride && stringIsUrl(item.imageOverride)){

                // show_override = true;

                const timing_up = item.TimingUp ? new Date(item.TimingUp) : null;
                const timing_down = item.TimingDown ? new Date(item.TimingDown) : null;
                const now = new Date();
                let out_of_date_range = false;

                function isValidDate(d) {
                  return d instanceof Date && !isNaN(d);
                }

                //check for either up or down date out of range
                //Note: requirements specified that if timingDown is after timingUp then "Timing Up value becomes voided and only the Timing Down takes priority".
                if ((isValidDate(timing_up) && now < timing_up && (isValidDate(timing_down) && timing_up < timing_down)) || isValidDate(timing_down) && now > timing_down) {
                  // show_override = false;
                  // disable_link = true;
                  out_of_date_range = true;
                }
                // }

                // let img_src = show_override ? item.imageOverride : item.imageDefault;
                img_src = item.imageDefault;

                //validation
                if (item.description && cat_nav_items_count < 99 && !out_of_date_range) {

                  slider_valid = true;
                  cat_nav_items_count++;


                  //add Sirv parameters
                  if (img_src && img_src.indexOf('sirv') > 0) {
                    if (img_src.indexOf('?') > 0) {
                      // console.log(img_src.substring(0, img_src.indexOf('?')));
                      img_src = img_src.substring(0, img_src.indexOf('?'));
                    }
                  }
                  const description_2 = item.description_2 ? "<br>" + item.description_2 : "";
                  const description_2_tagging = item.description_2 ? item.description_2 : "";
                  const description_colour = item.description_colour ? "color:" + item.description_colour : "";
                  const link_html = item.redirectURL && !disable_link ? '<a class="cat-nav__link" href="' + item.redirectURL + '" style="' + description_colour + '" onclick="catRichNavTagging.tileClick(\'' + item.description + ' ' + description_2_tagging + '\' , ' + cat_nav_items_count + ')">' : '<span class="cat-nav__link cat-nav__link--disabled" style="' + description_colour + '">';
                  const link_html_close = item.redirectURL && !disable_link ? '</a>' : "</span>";
                  const alt_text = item.imageAlt ? item.imageAlt : "";
                  const chevron_or_not = item.redirectURL && !disable_link ? '<span class="hidden-xs">&nbsp;&gt;</span>' : "";

                  img_src = img_src + "?w=210&h=180&canvas.width=210&canvas.height=180&canvas.opacity=0&q=70";
                  cat_nav_items +=  `<div class="cat-nav__tile text-center">` +
                                      link_html +
                                        `<div class="cat-nav__image-wrap">
                                          <img class="cat-nav__image lazy" alt="` + alt_text + `" data-src="` + img_src + `" width="105" height="90">
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="cat-nav__tile-title text-medium">` + item.description + description_2 + `</div>` +
                                      link_html_close +
                                    `</div>`;
                }
              }
            }
          }
          if (slider_valid) {
            cat_nav_title = json.slider_title ? json.slider_title : "";
            cat_bg = json.slider_background ? json.slider_background : "";
            cat_title_colour = json.slider_title_colour ? json.slider_title_colour : "";
            goRender();
          } else {
            console.log("rich navigation: manual data not valid");
            cat_nav_items = "";
            cat_nav_items_count=0;
            // loadDefault();
          }
        }
      })
      // .catch( error => {
      //   // loadDefault();
      //   console.error(`error ${error}`);
      // })
  }


  function loadDefault() {

    //get L2 data for L1, otherwise L3 data
    const L_type_data = page_type < 2 ? 2 : 3;

    const default_data_url = "https://rich-navigation.firebaseio.com/L" + L_type_data + "_Data/" + cat_to_get_default_url +"/L" + L_type_data + "_Categories.json"; //TEST
    console.log({default_data_url});
    fetch(default_data_url)
      .then(response => {
        if(!response.ok) {
          throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
        }
        return response.json();
      })
      .then(json => {
// json = test_data;
      // console.table(json);
        console.log(json);
      //   cat_nav_items += `<li class="cat-nav__tile text-center">

      // <a id="CategoriesESpotImgLink_716139900_4" href="https://www.thegoodguys.com.au/ClickInfo?evtype=CpgnClick&amp;mpe_id=716139900&amp;intv_id=716501459&amp;storeId=900&amp;URL=https%3a%2f%2fwww.thegoodguys.com.au%2ffridge-sale" aria-label="Fridge Sale" title="Fridge Sale" onclick="dataLayer.push({'event': 'TGGCATLP1GAEvent','TGGCATLPEventCategory':'Product Category L1:Fridges &amp; Freezers','TGGCATLPEventAction':'Product Category L2:','TGGCATLPEventLabel':'Product Category L3:, tile position : 4'});" onfocus="dojo.style('CategoriesESpotImgLink_716139900_4', 'outline', 'none'); 
      //       if (dojo.isChrome) {dojo.style('CategoryImage_716139900_4', 'border', '1px solid orange');} 
      //       else {dojo.style('CategoryImage_716139900_4', 'border', '1px dotted gray');}" onblur="dojo.style('CategoryImage_716139900_4', 'border', '1px solid transparent');">

      //   <div class="cat-nav__image-wrap">
      //     <img class="cat-nav__image" alt="Fridge Sale" src="https://thegoodguys.sirv.com/products/TopDeals/top-deals.png">
      //   </div>
      
      
      //   <div class="cat-nav__tile-title text-medium">Top ` + cat_to_get_default + ` Deals</div>
      // </a>

      //   </li>`;
        for (item of json) {
          // console.log(item);

          cat_nav_items_count++;
          
          let img_src = item.thumbnail;

          //add Sirv parameters
          if (img_src && img_src.indexOf('sirv') > 0) {
            if (img_src.indexOf('?') > 0) {
              // console.log(img_src.substring(0, img_src.indexOf('?')));
              img_src = img_src.substring(0, img_src.indexOf('?'));
            }
          }
          img_src = img_src + "?canvas.width=180&canvas.height=154&w=180&h=154&q=50";
          cat_nav_items +=  `<div class="cat-nav__tile text-center">
                              <a href="` + item.URL + `">
                                <div class="cat-nav__image-wrap">
                                  <img class="cat-nav__image lazy" alt="" data-src="` + img_src + `" width="90" height="77">
                                </div>
                                <div class="cat-nav__tile-title text-medium">` + item.name + `</div>
                              </a>
                            </div>`;
        }


        if (json.length) {
          cat_nav_title = 'Shop ' + cat_to_get_default + ' by Product Type';
          goRender()
        }
      })
      .catch( error => {
        console.error(`error ${error}`);
      })
  }


  let video_html = "";
  let video_slider = false;

  function goRender(){

    //manually disable video slider
    video_html = "";
    video_slider = true;

    document.getElementById('rich-navigation').style.display = 'block';

    const right_panel_classes = video_slider ? " cat-nav--floated-right col-md-12 col-lg-12 padd-0" : "";

    cat_nav_title = cat_nav_title ? cat_nav_title : 'Shop ' + getBreadcrumbInfo().category_name + ' by Product Type';

    const cat_title_colour_html = cat_title_colour ? ' style="color:' + cat_title_colour + '"' : '';

    const cat_nav_title_html = '<h2 class="cat-nav__title padd-left-15 padd-right-15 padd-top-0 marg-0 text-size-115"' + cat_title_colour_html + '>' + cat_nav_title + '</h2>';

    const cat_nav_html = '<div class="cat-nav' + right_panel_classes + '"><nav class="padd-top-10">' + cat_nav_title_html + '<div class="cat-nav__slider line-height-sml">' + cat_nav_items + '</div></nav></div>';

    const all_html = cat_nav_html + video_html;

    document.getElementById('rich-navigation-main').innerHTML = all_html;

    var catRichNavlazyLoadInstance = new LazyLoad({
      unobserve_entered:true
    });
    catRichNavlazyLoadInstance.update();

    const $carousel = $('.cat-nav__slider');

    const mediaQuery = window.matchMedia('(min-width: 992px)');

    function handleTabletChange(e) {
      if (e.matches) {
        console.log("slick");
        initialiseSlickSlide();
      //} else {
        //const el = document.querySelector('.cat-nav__slider');
        //if($(el).hasClass('slick-initialized')){
          //console.log("unslick");
          //$(el).slick('unslick'); just doesn't work
        //}
      }
    }

    mediaQuery.addEventListener('change', handleTabletChange);

    handleTabletChange(mediaQuery);
  

    // initialiseSlickSlide();
    
    // set mobile/tablet slider width
    function initialiseSlickSlide() {
      // debugger;

      //avoiding using slick if unnessary so we can position tiles with flexbox
      // if ($(window).width() >= 1200){
        if (cat_nav_items_count > 4) {
          runSlider(5);
        }
      // } else if (cat_nav_items_count > 5) {
      //   runSlider(5);
      // }

      function runSlider(max_slides) {
        $carousel.slick({
            infinite: false,
            slidesToShow: max_slides,
            slidesToScroll: max_slides,
            arrows: true,
            vertical:false,
            respondTo: 'slider',
            prevArrow: "<span class='cat-nav__prev slick-arrow' style='display: block;' onClick='window.catRichNavTagging.leftArrowClick();'><i class='ggdsicon-angle-left'></i></span>",
            nextArrow: "<span class='cat-nav__next slick-arrow' style='display: block;' onClick='window.catRichNavTagging.rightArrowClick();'><i class='ggdsicon-angle-right'></i></span>",
            responsive: [
                {
                    breakpoint: 700,
                    settings: {
                      slidesToShow: 4,
                      slidesToScroll: 4
                    }
                }
            ]
        })
      }
    }
    window.catRichNavTagging = {}
    window.catRichNavTagging.tileClick = function(description, position){
      this.fireTaggingEvent({'event': 'category_nav_widget','TGGEventCategory':'Category Nav Widget','TGGEventAction': 'Category - ' + window.location.href + ", L" + getBreadcrumbInfo().page_type,'TGGEventLabel': description + ", Position: " + position});
    }
    window.catRichNavTagging.leftArrowClick = function(){
      this.fireTaggingEvent({'event': 'category_nav_widget','TGGEventCategory':'Category Nav Widget','TGGEventAction':'Category - Scroll to Browse' ,'TGGEventLabel':'Arrow Prev'});
    }
    window.catRichNavTagging.rightArrowClick = function(){
      this.fireTaggingEvent({'event': 'category_nav_widget','TGGEventCategory':'Category Nav Widget','TGGEventAction':'Category - Scroll to Browse' ,'TGGEventLabel':'Arrow Next'});
    }
    window.catRichNavTagging.fireTaggingEvent = function(json) {
      // console.log(json);
      dataLayer.push(json);
    }
  }
}();
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    lazyLoadInstance.update();
  
    $(document).ready(function () {
        let pdfModalLinks = document.getElementsByClassName("load-pdf");
        let pdfLoader = function () {
            let modalId = this.getAttribute("data-target").substring(1);
            let targetModal = document.getElementById(modalId);
            let targetIframes = targetModal.querySelectorAll("iframe[pdf-src]");
            Array.from(targetIframes).forEach(function (targetIframe) {
                targetIframe.setAttribute("src", targetIframe.getAttribute('pdf-src'));
            });
        };
        Array.from(pdfModalLinks).forEach(function (pdfModalLink) {
            pdfModalLink.addEventListener('click', pdfLoader);
        });
  
        // remove shop now button on cat espot when on clickthrough location
        let pathName = window.location.href;
        let ctaBtnLink = 'no page';
        if (document.getElementById("half-category-espot-link")) {
            ctaBtnLink = document.getElementById("half-category-espot-link").href;
        }
        if (pathName == ctaBtnLink) {
            $('#half-category-espot-link').removeAttr("href");
            $('#half-category-espot-link .cta-btn').hide();
        }  
    });
  </script>

  <style>
    .ggds .timed-footer-disclaimer {
        display: none;

  <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // scheduling script
        var current_time_for_footer_disclaimer = new Date();
        var timedFd = $(".timed-footer-disclaimer");
        for (var i = 0; i < timedFd.length; i++) {
            var start_date_fd = new Date(timedFd[i].getAttribute("startFd"));
            var end_date_fd = new Date(timedFd[i].getAttribute("endFd"));
            if ((current_time_for_footer_disclaimer < end_date_fd) && (current_time_for_footer_disclaimer > start_date_fd)) {
                $(timedFd[i]).toggle();
            } else {
                $(timedFd[i]).remove();
            }
        }
    });
  </script>

					const BASEFQDN = 'https://wch.thegoodguys.com.au';
					const baseTenantAPIURL = BASEFQDN + "/api/";
					const deliveryRenderURL = baseTenantAPIURL + "delivery/v1/rendering/context/" + ''
					const authURL = baseTenantAPIURL + "authoring/v1/content/" + ''
					const assetURL = baseTenantAPIURL + "authoring/v1/assets/" + ''
					const resourceURL = BASEFQDN +"/<TENANT_ID>";
					const resourcesURL = baseTenantAPIURL + "authoring/v1/resources/" + ''
					var doLogin = false;
					var qs = "?include=links"
					var WCHWithCredentials = doLogin;
				</script>
  			
<script type="text/javascript">
var loggedIn = false;
// Make an HTTP request using the attribute value as the file name
function doWCHLogin() {
if (loggedIn == false) {
    console.log("not logged in");
    
    var gotResponse = false;
    var xhttpLogin = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhttpLogin.withCredentials = WCHWithCredentials;
    xhttpLogin.onload = function() {
      if (xhttpLogin.status == 200 || xhttpLogin.status == 204) {
        // Logged in OK
        //alert("Login: " + xhttpLogin.responseText);
        console.log('Login:' + xhttpLogin.responseText);
        loggedIn = true;
      } else {
        // Some error
        //alert("Unable to login: " + xhttpLogin.responseText);
         console.log('Unable to login:' + xhttpLogin.responseText);
      }
      gotResponse = true;
    }
    // xhttpLogin.open("GET", baseTenantAPIURL + "/login/v1/basicauth", false, "apikey", "a1LBNSoIroVfMBpVJTifUw5dfvbINpsUc4LTzjl_i-Wl");
    xhttpLogin.open("GET", baseTenantAPIURL + "login/v1/basicauth", false);

    console.log("logging in");
    xhttpLogin.setRequestHeader("Authorization", "Basic " + btoa(WCHUsername + ":" + WCHPassword));
    xhttpLogin.send();
    loggedIn = true;
    // while (gotResponse == false) {
      // wait of onLoad() to finish
      // if (gotResponse == true) { break; }
    // }
  }
}
</script>


<!-- Include WCH HTML from a Content reference --><!-- Looks for all div's with Arribute "wch-include-html" and replaces innerHTML with value from the referenced content.  --><!-- The reference content is called by AJAX and the returning JSON is parsed to get the content type and value -->
<script type="text/javascript">
dojo.require("dojo.html");

function wchlogin() {
      return request({uri: loginURL, json:true,
             auth:{"user":WCHUsername,"pass":WCHPassword,"endImmediately": true}});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function includeWCHHTML2(){
  var z, i, elmnt, attrFile, file, xhttp, requestFQDN;
  if(isIE() && doLogin){
          alert("IE is not supported for preview of WCH content");
          return;
  }
  // Loop through a collection of all HTML elements:
  z = document.getElementsByTagName("*");
  for (i = 0; i < z.length; i++) {
    elmnt = z[i];
    // Search for elements with a certain atrribute:
    var attrFile = elmnt.getAttribute("wch-include-html");
    if (attrFile) {
      // Found an element, process it
      file = deliveryRenderURL + attrFile;
      authFile = authURL + attrFile  + qs;
      // Requesting content, check for if login required
      if (doLogin == true) {
        if (loggedIn == false) {
          // Login required and not logged in, so attempt API login, then proceed
          doWCHLogin();
        }
         getItem(authFile, "content", elmnt);
      } else {
        if(isIE()){
          getItem_ie(file, "content", elmnt);
        } else { 
          getItem(file, "content", elmnt);
        }
      }
    }
  }  
}
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
  var tggAssetAttrName = "file";  //ST value
  var tggShortHTMLName = "html";      //ST and TGG value
  //var tggAssetAttrName = "file";    //TGG value
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
function getItem(dFile, type, elem, isRetry){
  $(elem).removeAttr("wch-include-html");  //remove the wch-include-html attribute so that the element is only processed once
  if(!doLogin){  //live site
    if(dFile.includes("dxresources")){  
      fetch(dFile, {method:'GET'}).
      then(text => response.text()).
      then(getItemCallBack(text));
    } else {
      fetch(dFile,  {method:'GET'}).
      then(response => response.json()).
      then(json => {
        if(json.elements.html){
          getItemCallBack({"html":json.elements.html.value}, elem, false);
        } else if(json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].asset){
          fetch(BASEFQDN + json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].url, {method:'GET'}).
          then(response => response.text()).
          then(text => {
            var obj = {"html":text};
            getItemCallBack(obj, elem, false)
          })
          .catch(function(error){
            console.log('error b',error);
          })
        }
        })
      .catch(function(error){
        console.log('error url:' + dFile,error);
      })

    }
  } else {  //preview site
  //if on preview site, check for draft available:
    fetch(dFile, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
    then(response => response.json()).
      then(json => {
        if(json.errors && isRetry){
          getItemCallBack({"html":"Item could not be found"}, elem, true)
          return;
        }
        if(json.errors && !isRetry){
          //We have some errors in the json, so item may still be in draft. 
          var dArr = dFile.split("?");
          dFileN = dArr[0] + ":draft?" + dArr[1];
          getItem(dFileN,type, elem, true);
          return;
        }
        if(json.status=="draft"){
          //we have the draft item - no published item exists yet
          if(json.elements[tggShortHTMLName] && json.elements[tggShortHTMLName].elementType=="text"){
              //this a short html piece of content
              getItemCallBack({"html":json.elements[tggShortHTMLName].value}, elem, true)
            } else {
              //fetch the asset
              let urlB = assetURL + json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].asset.id + ":draft";
              fetch(urlB, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
              then(response => response.json()).
              then(json => {
                //Fetch the html from the asset
                let urlC = resourcesURL + json.resource;
                fetch(urlC, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
                then(response => response.text()).
                then(text => {
                  var obj = {"html":text};
                  getItemCallBack(obj, elem, true)
                });
              }); 
            }
        } else if(json.links.draft){
          let urlA = baseTenantAPIURL + json.links.draft.href;
          fetch(urlA, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
          then(response => response.json()).
          then(json => {
            if(json.elements[tggShortHTMLName] && json.elements[tggShortHTMLName].elementType=="text"){
              //this a short html piece of content
              getItemCallBack({"html":json.elements[tggShortHTMLName].value}, elem, true)
            } else {
              //fetch the asset
              let urlB = assetURL + json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].asset.id + "?projectId=draft";
              fetch(urlB, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
              then(response => response.json()).
              then(json => {
                //Fetch the html from the asset
                let urlC = resourcesURL + json.resource;
                fetch(urlC, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
                then(response => response.text()).
                then(text => {
                  var obj = {"html":text};
                  getItemCallBack(obj, elem, true)
                });
              }); 
            }
          });
        } else if(json.elements){
          //get the original asset
          if(json.elements[tggShortHTMLName] && json.elements[tggShortHTMLName].elementType=="text"){
              //this a short html piece of content
              getItemCallBack({"html":json.elements[tggShortHTMLName].value}, elem, false)
          } else {
      
            let urlD = assetURL + json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].asset.id;
            fetch(urlD, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
            then(response => response.json()).
            then(json => {
              //Fetch the html from the asset
              let urlE = resourcesURL + json.resource;
              fetch(urlE, {method:'GET', credentials: 'include'}).
              then(response => response.text()).
              then(text => {
                var obj = {"html":text};
                getItemCallBack(obj, elem, false)
              });
            }); 
          }
        }
      });
  }
}
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
//This is the IE version of the getItem function.  jQuery promises are used instead of ES6

  function getItem_ie(dFile, type, elem, isRetry){
    $(elem).removeAttr("wch-include-html");  //remove the wch-include-html attribute so that the element is only processed once
    var jqXHR = $.ajax({
      url: dFile,
      method: "GET"
    });
    if(dFile.indexOf("dxresources") > -1){  

    } else {
      jqXHR
      .done(function(json, status, xhr){
        if(json.elements.html){
          getItemCallBack({"html":json.elements.html.value}, elem, false);
        } else if(json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].asset){
          var jqXHR2 = $.ajax({
            url: BASEFQDN + json.elements[tggAssetAttrName].url,
            method: "GET"
          });
          jqXHR2
            .done(function(data2, status2, xhr2){
              var obj = {"html":data2};
              getItemCallBack(obj, elem, false);
            })     
            .fail(function(xhr2){
                console.log('error callback', xhr2);
            }) 
        }        
      })
      .fail(function(xhr){
        console.log('error callback', xhr);
      })  
    }
  }
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
function getItemCallBack(content, elmnt, isDraft){
  if(content.html){
    elmnt.innerHTML = content.html;
  } else {
      
  }
  // remove the attribute, and call this function once more
  elmnt.removeAttribute("wch-include-html");
  if(isDraft){
    $(elmnt).addClass("wch-draft");
  }  
  var scriptElement = elmnt.getElementsByTagName("script");
  for(var n=0; n<scriptElement.length; n++){
    eval(scriptElement[n].innerHTML);
  } 
  includeWCHHTML2(); 
}
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
function isIE() {
  var ms_ie = false;
  var ua = window.navigator.userAgent; 
  var old_ie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
  var new_ie = ua.indexOf('Trident/');

  if ((old_ie > -1) || (new_ie > -1)) {
      return true;
  }
  return false;
}

</script>

	$(document).ready(function(){
		includeWCHHTML2();
	});
</script>
